INNER JOIN [Job].[Companies] AS [c] ON [m].[CompanyId] = [c].[CompanyId]

INNER JOIN [Job].[Companies] AS [c] ON [m].[CompanyId] = [c].[CompanyId]
INNER JOIN [Job].[Jobs] AS [j] ON [m].[JobId] = [j].[JobId]

FROM [Common].[Message] AS [m]
